    <script language="" type="text/javascript">
        function ShowProvinces() {
            $("#ctl00_flotingMenu").css('display', 'block');
            document.getElementById('dnn_ctr474_LocationBox_DrpRedius').style.visibility = 'hidden';
            return false;
        }

        function HideProvinces(dropdown) {            
            $(".overlayDiv").css('display', 'none');            
            document.getElementById('dnn_ctr474_LocationBox_DrpRedius').style.visibility = 'visible';
            return false;
        }
        $(document).ready(function () { $('.ui-pcode').focus(function () { if ($.trim($(this).val()).toLowerCase() == 'postal code') { $(this).val(''); } }).blur(function () { if ($.trim($(this).val()).length == 0 && $.trim($(this).val()) == '') { $(this).val('Postal Code') } }); });
        


		function noNumbers(c, e) {
		var keynum; var keychar; var numcheck; varstring = c.value;
		if (window.event) { keynum = e.keyCode } else if (e.which) { keynum = e.which }
		keychar = String.fromCharCode(keynum);

		if (keynum) {
			if (keynum == 8) { c.focus(); return true }
			if (varstring.length == 3) { c.value = c.value + " " } 
		varstring = c.value; if (varstring.length == 1 || varstring.length == 4 || varstring.length == 6) { return NumericValOnly(keychar) } if (varstring.length == 0 || varstring.length == 2 || varstring.length == 5) { return CheracterValOnly(keychar) } for (J = 0; J < varstring.length; J++) { if (J == 3) { if (keynum == 32) { c.focus(); return true } } } } else { c.focus() } } function NumericValOnly(strChar) { var strValidChars = "0123456789"; if (strValidChars.indexOf(strChar) == -1) { return false } } function CheracterValOnly(strChar) { var strValidChars = "abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ"; if (strValidChars.indexOf(strChar) == -1) { return false } } function OpenSearchResult(url) { if (top === self) { window.location = url } else { window.parent.location = url } }


    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $.fn.MainNavigationController = function () {            
            this.each(function () {
                var $items = $('.navbar li', this);
                $items.bind('mouseenter', items_Over).bind('mouseleave', items_Out);
                $('.main-menu-window').bind('mouseenter', menu_Over).bind('mouseleave', menu_Out);
                function items_Over(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $(this).addClass('hover');
                    $('.main-menu-window').hide();
                    if ($(this).attr('data-window') != '') {
                        $('#' + $(this).attr('data-window')).show();
                    }
                }

                function items_Out(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $('.main-menu-window').hide();
                    $(this).removeClass('hover');
                }
                function menu_Over(e) {
                    $(this).show();
                    var dataAttr = $('#' + $(this).attr('data-menuitem'));
                    if (dataAttr != '') {
                        $(dataAttr).addClass('hover');
                    }
                }

                function menu_Out(e) {
                    $(this).hide();
                    var dataAttr = $('#' + $(this).attr('data-menuitem'));
                    if (dataAttr != '') {
                        $(dataAttr).removeClass('hover');
                    }
                }
            });
        };
        $('#main-header').MainNavigationController();
    });
            
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    function NavigateSort(sortMethod) {
        var str = document.getElementById('dnn_ctr472_SearchResult_GridHeader2_hidSortLinkPattern').value;
        window.location = str.replace("___SORTMETHOD___", sortMethod).toLowerCase();
    }

    function NavigatePageSize(pageSize) {
        var str = document.getElementById('dnn_ctr472_SearchResult_GridHeader2_hidPageSizeLinkPattern').value;
        window.location = str.replace("___PAGESIZE___", pageSize).toLowerCase();
    }

</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    function DeleteScrapbook(id) {
        var webMethod = '/DesktopModules/MLFx.DNNModule.Wheels.SearchResult/Services.asmx/DeleteScrapbook';
        var parameters = "{'ID':'" + id + "'}"

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: webMethod,
            data: parameters,
            contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
            dataType: "json",
            success: function () {
                window.location = window.location;
            }
        });
    }
</script>
